Our catalog with **#20241123** (Catalog version **3.4.281** ) is available to our **Easy2Patch** customers.

This week, **51** software updates are provided in the E2P catalog. We support **430** products of **287** individual manufacturers in total. We are updating **560** products with 32/64-bit and language options.

***Note:*** *VirusTotal and Kaspersky Opentip scans are the responsibility of the manufacturer. E2P Bilisim has no responsibility or liability for the virus scanning results of the files.*

For Software Updater, we’ve also tweaked it so that it now cleans up installers downloaded during the updating process more effectively.

> Version 12.7.8 -- Nov 15, 2024 \* Filters: Allow environment variables in Filters. \* Snapshots: Fixed GS does not delete VSS snapshots if the job is Stopped by User. \* CC-Runner: Fixed CC-runner does not report anything if an OFC job can't start. \* Account Setup dialog: Do not pre-fill password, for security reasons.

> 12.2.0 – 2024-11-04 Removed Visual Studio build files have been removed. CMake is now the only supported build system on Windows. Added Support for building the SWIG-generated PHP language bindings has been integrated into the CMake build system. This is controllable by the -DENABLE\_PHP={AUTO|ON|OFF} option.

> [Windows] v15.59.5 New features The Remote Support window has been redesigned to a layout inspired by the Classic interface. You can now clearly distinguish if you want to receive or provide remote control. Session codes and the TeamViewer ID/password are both prominently displayed along with a list of recent connections. Supporters can now join a session and wait for the user in a dedicated waiting room. This enhanced waiting room allows supporters to easily view and copy session details while awaiting connection with the user.
